○011782○消去
●011782●消去

○011783○I don't have any memories of my family.
●011783●我并没有和家庭有关的记忆。

○011784○By the time I was old enough to understand the concept, I was already living in my uncle's house.
●011784●等我记事的时候，已经在母亲的哥哥家生活了。

○011785○That uncle, my foster father, had two children.
●011785●继父有两个孩子。

○011786○My foster brother and sister. 
●011786●义兄和义妹。

○011787○Naturally, their parents showered their real children with affection.
●011787●身为双亲，自然会将爱倾注到自己的孩子身上。

○011788○They treated me like an unseemly boil in the family. There was always a wall between us.
●011788●我就好像是个外人一样，和他们之间总是隔着一堵屏障。

○011789○I couldn't bring myself to call them 'Mom' and 'Dad' like their real children did.
●011789●我不能像那两个孩子一样，叫他们『爸爸』和『妈妈』。

○011790○Even as a child, I think I was aware of that wall.
●011790●就算是个孩子，似乎也已经感受到了这堵『屏障』。

○011791○As I grew older, still devoid of even a fragment of honesty regarding my own feelings, I drifted away from them even further.
●011791●丢失了这份坦率的碎片的我，随着年龄的增长，和他们更加疏远了。

○011792○I was left to watch over the house alone time after time.
●011792●总是被一个人留在家里看家。

○011793○When they left me alone to travel as a family, I would take the money they left for my expenses and go out to cheap beef bowl restaurants on my own.
●011793●也无法参加家庭旅行，只能拿着他们留下的伙食费，去吃便宜的牛肉盖饭。

○011794○There was no way I'd turn out normally, being raised in an environment like that.
●011794●在这种环境下，我是不可能好好成长的。

○011795○My life had never been on track at all.
●011795●从最开始，就没能坐上轨道。

○011796○It jumped the rails from the very beginning.
●011796●从最开始，就已经偏离了路线。

○011797○To distance myself from those parents, I enrolled in a boarding school by means of a sports recommendation. 
●011797●为了和这样的父母分开，我决定通过体育特招推荐，进入完全寄宿制的高中。

○011798○When I learned that I'd been accepted into the program, I clenched my fists in victory.
●011798●当我得知自己得到了推荐名额之后，不禁握紧了拳头。

○011799○'Yes,' I thought. 'I can finally escape them.'
●011799●好，可以逃离这里了。

○011800○I only joined the little league in the first place for the sake of spending as little time at home as possible.
●011800●最初加入小型联盟赛，也只是为了尽量减少待在家里的时间。

○011801○That was the only reason why I started playing baseball.
●011801●开始打棒球的理由，仅此而已。

○011802○I handled almost all of the paperwork and formalities on my own.
●011802●所有的手续几乎都是我一个人办的。

○011803○I only needed my parents to sign their names on the documentation, but even asking for that felt humiliating.
●011803●只需要拜托他们在文件上签名，但仅仅是这样就已经觉得很屈辱了。

○011804○After entering high school, I found myself increasingly devoted to baseball.
●011804●在进入高中之后，我发现自己越来越热爱棒球了。

○011805○If I could get good enough at it, I'd be able to get into college regardless of my academic ability. That fact drove me even further.
●011805●只要棒球打得够好，就算不用学习也能考上大学。所以我更加沉浸了。

○011806○I practiced desperately, pushing myself as hard as I could.
●011806●拼命地努力练习。

○011807○At some point along the way, playing baseball became my life itself.
●011807●不知道什么时候，打棒球已经变成活着本身了。

○011808○People should live for the sake of living.
●011808●人应当为了生活而活着。

○011809○Living for the sake of baseball can't possibly be right.
●011809●为了打棒球而活着是不行的。

○011810○It was almost like I'd become a robot, built solely to play baseball.
●011810●我好像已经变成了一个机器人，为了打棒球而被制造出来。

○011811○I'd lost something important to myself as a human being.
●011811●我失去了作为一个人类而言重要的东西。

○011812○Or, maybe I'd never had that something to begin with.
●011812●不，也许原本就没有那样的东西。

○011813○One day, a dog wandered into the school grounds.
●011813●有一天，一条狗在学校的操场上迷路了。

○011814○It didn't have a collar. A stray. 
●011814●因为有项圈，所以是家养的狗。

○011815○It was still there the next day.
●011815●第二天也在。

○011816○It must have stayed around, even after we went back to the dorm.
●011816●好像在我们回到了宿舍之后，依然还留在那里。

○011817○It seemed quite docile, and sat in the same spot without even walking around, constantly wagging its tail.
●011817●看起来是条相当温顺的狗，甚至不来回走动，就坐在同一个地方，不停地摇着尾巴。

○011818○The club manager decided that it was a problem.
●011818●球队经理觉得这是个问题。

○011819○She said we should search for its owner.
●011819●决定去寻找它的主人。

○011820○We made fliers with its picture on them, which we hung up on utility poles and passed out in the nearby neighborhoods. 
●011820●我们制作了传单，贴在了电线杆上，分发给附近的人家。

○011821○I was put in charge of an area, and told to help as well. 
●011821●我也被安排了一片负责区域，要求帮忙干活。

○011822○But I couldn't even begin to understand the point of doing something like that.
●011822●我完全理解不了这种行为有什么意义。

○011823○If I find that dog's owner, would it go on my academic record?
●011823●就算找到了狗的主人的话，能够记录到档案上吗？

○011824○Could I tell the story to cast myself in a good light during job interviews?
●011824●在找工作面试的时候，能够用这个故事去宣传自己吗？

○011825○Our coach told us that there were no downsides to doing a good deed.
●011825●教练说做好事不需要理由。

○011826○But from my perspective, it was just getting in the way of our practice.
●011826●但在我看来，只是在妨碍我们练习而已。

○011827○Days passed by, but there was still no sign of its owner. 
●011827●过了好多天，也没能找到它的主人。

○011828○During that period, we came to a realization. 
●011828●在这期间，我们才意识到。

○011829○The dog couldn't walk properly. 
●011829●这条狗没法正常走路。

○011830○It looked like it had been injured, and it dragged one leg along limply.
●011830●好像受伤了，行走的时候拖着一只脚。

○011831○Our manager took it to a veterinary clinic. 
●011831●经理带着这条狗去了兽医医院。

○011832○They examined it, and told her that it wasn't going to heal.
●011832●诊断结果是『无法治疗』。

○011833○The whole baseball club was called together for a meeting about what we would do with the dog. Once again, I couldn't even begin to see the point.
●011833●同样完全无法理解的是，棒球部为了讨论如何处理这条狗而展开了回忆。

○011834○Who gives a crap, right? Why can't we just practice? Our careers and futures are on the line here, you know?
●011834●这种事怎样都无所谓吧？练习呢？那可是关系到我们的前途和未来的吧？

○011835○I was filled with doubts.
●011835●我整个人充满了疑问。

○011836○I imagined that the dog's owner couldn't bear to watch it suffer anymore, and abandoned it at a school on purpose, hoping to shove it off on someone else.
●011836●狗的主人肯定是因为无法目睹它痛苦的样子，为了能让别人接盘照顾，才故意扔到学校的。

○011837○Then our coach came to an unfathomable conclusion. 
●011837●然后教练和部员们得出了一个难以理解的结论。

○011838○The baseball club would look after it.
●011838●由棒球部来照顾它。

○011839○Huh? What? [Why?]
●011839●哈啊？为什么？Why?

○011840○At that point, I was still putting on a facade of being a normal person.
●011840●那个时候的我，还戴着正常人的面具。

○011841○So I just went with the flow, and agreed with the group.
●011841●所以，我就随波逐流地同意了。

○011842○But it threw the baseball club's practice into complete disorder.
●011842●但是，棒球部的练习被彻底打乱了。

○011843○Someone was always busy looking after the dog.
●011843●大家都在意着照顾狗的事情。

○011844○It was plain to see that everyone's motivation to up their game had dropped dramatically.
●011844●打棒球的士气明显地低落了下来。

○011845○Near the end, my teammates started spending their time planning to make a wheeled prosthesis to help the dog walk properly.
●011845●在接近尾声的时候，甚至计划起了制作带轮子的假肢，从而能让那条狗正常走路。

○011846○What the hell?
●011846●怎么回事啊。

○011847○It was bringing the whole club down.
●011847●明显有害无益。

○011848○It was obvious it didn't have long to live, considering how frail it was.
●011848●看它虚弱的样子，显然已经活不了多久了。

○011849○Why did a useless creature like that have to steal the motivation of my entire baseball team?
●011849●为什么要让这种无聊的存在，夺走我们整个棒球部的士气啊。

○011850○Have you people lost your minds?
●011850●大家的理智呢？

○011851○There's something wrong with this, right? 
●011851●绝对很奇怪。

○011852○Have they been bewitched by some sort of mass hypnosis?
●011852●难道是因为某种集体催眠术吗？

○011853○That's why I decided to bring them to their senses.
●011853●所以，我决定让他们清醒过来。

○011854○I took action before the prosthetic could be completed. 
●011854●我在假肢制作完成之前就采取了行动。

○011855○It was simple.
●011855●很简单。

○011856○I just had to quietly take it out somewhere far away and leave it there, just like its old owner had done.
●011856●只要和它原来的主人一样，悄悄地把它扔的远远的就行了。

○011857○Since it could hardly walk, it wouldn't be able to make its way back.
●011857●它又不能正常行走，所以回不来的。

○011858○After everyone else fell asleep, I picked up the dog and slipped out of the school with it.
●011858●我趁着其他人睡着了之后，抱起了狗，从学校里溜了出去。

○011859○I had to carry it far away, past where we'd distributed the fliers. That way no one would ever find out.
●011859●必须要带到比传单的散发范围更远的地方才行。这是保证不会暴露的必要条件。

○011860○I climbed up a mountain, into the woods. I kept walking, deep enough I could just barely make out the light from the nearby houses.
●011860●我爬到了山上，走进了树林，走到了勉强才能看到民房的灯光的地方。

○011861○Eventually, I was so deep I could barely see at all. It felt like I might get lost myself.
●011861●深入到这种地方的话，如果没有灯光，就是自己也会迷路的。

○011862○I sliced off its collar with a box cutter. Even if someone found it, to them, it'd just be a stray.
●011862●我用刀割断了它的项圈，这样即使有人发现了，也会把它当成野狗。

○011863○My work carefully completed, I went back home.
●011863●顺利地结束这件事，然后踏上归途。

○011864○The frustration I'd felt recently had kept me from sleeping well, but that night, I slept soundly for the first time in days.
●011864●虽然最近常常因为焦躁而睡眠不足，但那天晚上却睡得很舒服。

○011865○However, the next day, I was immediately outed as the culprit.
●011865●但是，第二天，我很快就被发现是犯人了。

●011866●为什么？
